## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x6D12 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[2] = Work_Zone[5]
  1: 0x6D17 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()

     0xCA29 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[21] = 403*
     0xCA2E [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[22] = 0*
     0xCA33 [0x01] GOTO 0xCA56
     0xCA36 [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[23] == 4*) GOTO 0xCA46
     0xCA3E [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[21] = 454*
     0xCA43 [0x01] GOTO 0xCA56
     0xCA46 [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[23] == 5*) GOTO 0xCA56
     0xCA4E [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[21] = 455*
     0xCA53 [0x01] GOTO 0xCA56
     0xCA56 [0x1B] RETURN
```
